| <span data-ttu-id="d5b54-441">進入</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b54-441">Entry</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="d5b54-442">值</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d5b54-442">Value</span></span> |
